GT Equivalence Verification (PO18)

GT: -beta*sin(x)*v - omega0**c0*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(x,t,v)= -0.583656039990477\, v\sin(x)\;-\;1.81264753578235\,x.
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (after choosing its free constants, and possibly restricting to a plausible continuous domain) to produce **exactly** a linear-in-\(x\) term with coefficient \(-1.8126...\), plus a \(v\sin(x)\) term with coefficient \(-0.5836...\), and **no** constant offset, no \(t\)-dependence, and no other \(x\)-nonlinearities.

Useful identity: \(\cos(x+\phi)=\sin(x)\) if \(\phi=-\pi/2\) (or \(\cos(x+\pi/2)=-\sin(x)\), etc.). So cosine forms can match the sine term by phase shift and sign.

---

### 1. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v*\cos(c3*x + c4) + c5*\cos(c6*t + c7)\)
To match GT, must remove constant and all \(t\)-dependence: set \(c5=0\). Also GT has no constant: set \(c1=0\).
Need \(c0 x = -1.8126475 x\) so \(c0=-1.8126475...\).
Need \(c2 v\cos(c3 x+c4) = -0.5836560\, v\sin(x)\). Choose \(c3=1\) and pick phase so cosine becomes sine: e.g. \(\cos(x-\pi/2)=\sin(x)\). Then set \(c4=-\pi/2\) and \(c2=-0.5836560...\).
Works globally. **Match.**

### 2. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v*\cos(c3*x + c4)\)
Set \(c1=0\). Set \(c0=-1.8126475...\). For trig term, same as above: \(c3=1\), \(c4=-\pi/2\), \(c2=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 3. \(c0*x^2 + c1*x + c2 + c3*v*\sin(c4*x + c5)\)
Must eliminate \(x^2\) and constant: set \(c0=0\), \(c2=0\).
Set \(c1=-1.8126475...\).
For sine term: need \(\sin(c4 x+c5)=\sin(x)\) up to sign; simplest \(c4=1,c5=0\), \(c3=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 4. \(c0*v*\sin(c1 + c2*x) + c3*x\)
Set \(c3=-1.8126475...\).
Need \(c0\sin(c1+c2 x)=-0.5836560\sin(x)\). Choose \(c2=1\), \(c1=0\), \(c0=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 5. \(c0*x*e^{c1 x} + c2 + c3*v*e^{c4 x}\cos(c5 x + c6)\)
To avoid non-polynomial \(x e^{c1x}\), set \(c1=0\) so term becomes \(c0 x\).
To avoid constant, set \(c2=0\).
To avoid \(e^{c4x}\) distortion, set \(c4=0\) so trig term is \(c3 v\cos(c5 x+c6)\).
Then match as in (1)/(2): set \(c0=-1.8126475...\), \(c5=1\), \(c6=-\pi/2\), \(c3=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 6. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*x^3\)
Eliminate \(x^3\): \(c5=0\). Eliminate constant: \(c1=0\). Then same as (2). **Match.**

### 7. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*e^{c6\sin(c7*x+c8)}\)
The exponential-of-sine term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Then reduce to (2) and match. **Match.**

### 8. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*v^3\)
Need no \(v^3\): set \(c5=0\). Need no constant: \(c1=0\). Then reduce to (2). **Match.**

### 9. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*\sin(c6*e^{c7 v}+c8)\)
Extra term depends on \(v\) only; GT has no such additive \(v\)-only term. Must remove it: set \(c5=0\). Also set \(c1=0\). Then reduce to (2). **Match.**

### 10. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*v\sin(c6*x+c7)\)
GT has only one \(v\)-trig term; we can set one of the two \(v\)-terms to zero. Easiest: set \(c5=0\), \(c1=0\), then reduce to (2). **Match.**
(Alternatively could set \(c2=0\) and use the sine term.)

### 11. \(c0*x + c1*v\cos(c2*x+c3)\)
No constant term—good. Match by cosine phase shift: set \(c0=-1.8126475...\). Need \(c1\cos(c2 x+c3)=-0.5836560\sin(x)\). Choose \(c2=1\), \(c3=-\pi/2\) so cosine becomes \(\sin(x)\), and \(c1=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 12. \(c0*x^2 + c1*x + c2*x e^{c3 x} + c4 + c5*v\sin(c6*x+c7)\)
Eliminate \(x^2\): \(c0=0\). Eliminate constant: \(c4=0\).
Need no \(x e^{c3x}\) beyond linear: set \(c2=0\) (or \(c3=0\) still leaves \(c2 x\) but then would interfere with \(c1 x\); easiest \(c2=0\)).
Then set \(c1=-1.8126475...\).
Set \(c6=1,c7=0,c5=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 13. \(c0*x + c1 + c2*v\cos(c3*x+c4) + c5*e^{c6 t}\sin(c7*x+c8)\)
GT has no \(t\)-dependence, so must remove last term: set \(c5=0\). Also set \(c1=0\). Then reduce to (2). **Match.**

### 14. \(c0*x + c1*v e^{c2 x} + c3*v + c4*v\log(c5 x^2+1) + c6*v x^3\)
GT’s \(v\)-dependence is \(v\sin(x)\), not \(v e^{c2x}\), \(v\), \(v\log(\cdot)\), or \(v x^3\). You can zero out unwanted terms by setting \(c1=c3=c4=c6=0\), leaving only \(c0 x\). But then you cannot produce the required \(v\sin(x)\) term. No other term can become \(v\sin(x)\) by parameter choice. **No match.**

### 15. \(c0*v + c1*v*x^2 + c2*x + c3*x + c4*v\sin(c5*x+c6)\)

Sine term: set \(c5=1,c6=0,c4=-0.5836560...\). **Match.**

### 16. Rational expression with denominator \((c1+x)\)
GT has no denominator. Only way is to make denominator constant by setting \(c1\) so that \(c1+x\) is constant—impossible. Alternatively, could try to cancel \((c1+x)\) by making numerator proportional to \((c1+x)\), but numerator is a sum of terms like \(x, x^2, v\sin(\cdot), v x\sin(\cdot)\) etc., not containing a free factor \((c1+x)\) globally. No parameter choice yields exact cancellation for all \(x\) on a continuous domain. **No match.**

### Candidate 1: c0*x + c1 + c2*v*cos(c3*x + c4) + c5*cos(c6*t + c7)
Has a cos(c6*t + c7) term. Setting c5=0 eliminates it, and c1=0. Then c0*x + c2*v*cos(c3*x + c4). With c3=1, c4=π/2: cos(x + π/2) = -sin(x). So this becomes c0*x + c2*v*(-sin(x)) = c0*x - c2*v*sin(x). ✓
**Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: c0*x + c1 + c2*v*cos(c3*x + c4)
Set c1=0, c3=1, c4=π/2: c0*x + c2*v*(-sin(x)). ✓

### Candidate 16: Complex rational expression with all terms divided by (c1+x).
Let me combine: [c0*x + c2*v*sin(c3+c4*x) + c5*v*x*sin(c4*x+c6) + c7*x + c8*x²]/(c1+x). This equals a rational function. GT = -0.5837*v*sin(x) - 1.8126*x. For this to equal GT, we need (c1+x)*(-0.5837*v*sin(x) - 1.8126*x) = numerator. The numerator would contain terms like c1*v*sin(x) and x*v*sin(x). The candidate has v*sin(c3+c4*x) and v*x*sin(c4*x+c6). Setting c4=1, c3=0, c6=0: v*sin(x) and v*x*sin(x). We need c1*(-0.5837)*v*sin(x) + (-0.5837)*x*v*sin(x) from the v*sin terms. The candidate provides c2*v*sin(x) + c5*v*x*sin(x). So c2 = -0.5837*c1 and c5 = -0.5837. For the x terms: -1.8126*c1*x - 1.8126*x² = (c0+c7)*x + c8*x². So c8 = -1.8126, c0+c7 = -1.8126*c1. This works! ✓
**Candidate 16 verdict: [MATCH]**
